 Due to these properties found in coconut water, doctors also recommend drinking coconut water
 1
 Raw coconut water contains electrolyte, chloride, calcium, potassium, magnesium, sodium and riboflavin
 ye sabhi poshak tatv garbhvatee mahila ke liye jaruri hote hai
 Also, its intake reduces the risk of dehydration and pregnant women are advised to drink more water anyway
 2
 Coconut water acts like a natural diuretics
